\"\"\necho \"\ud83d\udcf1 STEP 2: Creating BuilderPhone.tsx...\"\n\ncat > \"$BUILDER_DIR/BuilderPhone.tsx\" << 'BUILDERPHONE'\nimport React, { useState, useEffect, useRef, useCallback } from };\n\nconst BuilderPhone: React.FC<Props> = ({ phone, onChange, onNext, speak }) => {\n  const [localPhone, setLocalPhone] = useState(phone);\n  const [isListening, setIsListening] = useState(false);\n  const [transcript, setTranscript] = useState('');\n  const recognitionRef = useRef<any>(null);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    speak(\"Welcome builder! Please enter your phone number.\");\n  }, []);\n\n  // Voice recognition setup\n  useEffect(() => {\n    const SR = (window as any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\n    if (SR) {\n      recognitionRef.current = new SR();\n      recognitionRef.current.continuous = true;\n      recognitionRef.current.interimResults = true;\n      \n      recognitionRef.current.onresult = (event: any) => {\n        let text = '';\n        for (let i = event.resultIndex; i < event.results.length; i++) {\n          text += event.results[i][0].transcript;\n        }\n        setTranscript(text);\n        \n        if (event.results[event.resultIndex].isFinal) {\n          processVoice(text);\n        }\n      };\n    }\n  }, []);\n\n  const processVoice = useCallback((text: string) => {\n    const numberWords: Record<string, string> = {\n      'zero': '0', 'one': '1', 'two': '2', 'three': '3', 'four': '4',\n      'five': '5', 'six': '6', 'seven': '7', 'eight': '8', 'nine': '9', 'oh': '0'\n    };\n    \n    let processed = text.toLowerCase();\n    for (const [word, digit] of Object.entries(numberWords)) {\n      processed = processed.replace(new RegExp(`\\\\b${word}\\\\b`, 'g'), digit);\n    }\n    \n    const digits = processed.replace(/\\D/g, '');\n    if (digits.length > 0) {\n      const newPhone = (localPhone + digits).slice(0, 10);\n      setLocalPhone(newPhone);\n      onChange(newPhone);\n      \n      if (newPhone.length === 10) {\n        speak(\"Phone number complete. Click Send OTP to continue.\");\n      }\n    }\n  }, [localPhone, onChange, speak]);\n\n  const toggleListening = () => {\n    if (isListening) {\n      recognitionRef.current?.stop();\n      setIsListening(false);\n    } else {\n      recognitionRef.current?.start();\n      setIsListening(true);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const formatPhone = (p: string) => {\n    if (p.length <= 3) return p;\n    if (p.length <= 6) return `${p.slice(0,3)}-${p.slice(3)}`;\n    return `${p.slice(0,3)}-${p.slice(3,6)}-${p.slice(6)}`;\n  };\n\n  const handleChange = (value: string) => {\n    const digits = value.replace(/\\D/g, '').slice(0, 10);\n    setLocalPhone(digits);\n    onChange(digits);\n  };\n\n  const isValid = localPhone.length === 10;\n\n  return (\n    <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', alignItems: 'center', gap: 20 }}>\n      <span style={{ fontSize: '3em' }}>\ud83c\udfd7\ufe0f</span>\n      <h3 style={{ color: THEME.accent, margin: 0 }}>Builder Phone Number</h3>\n      <p style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: '0.9em', margin: 0 }}>\n        Say digits like \"seven zero three\" or type below\n      </p>\n\n      <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 10 }}>\n        <span style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: '1.2em' }}>+1</span>\n        <input\n          type=\"tel\"\n          value={formatPhone(localPhone)}\n          onChange={e => handleChange(e.target.value)}\n          placeholder=\"000-000-0000\"\n          style={{\n            padding: '16px 20px',\n            fontSize: '1.5em',\n            fontFamily: 'monospace',\n            background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)',\n            border: `2px solid ${isValid ? '#10b981' : THEME.accent}40`,\n            borderRadius: 12,\n            color: '#fff',\n            textAlign: 'center',\n            width: 220,\n            outline: 'none'\n          }}\n        />\n      </div>\n\n      {/* Voice Bar */}\n      <div style={{\n        width: '100%',\n        padding: 16,\n        background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)',\n        borderRadius: 16,\n        border: `2px solid ${isListening ? '#10b981' : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)'}`\n      }}>\n        <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 10, marginBottom: 12 }}>\n          <div style={{\n            width: 10, height: 10, borderRadius: '50%',\n            background: isListening ? '#10b981' : '#64748b',\n            animation: isListening ? 'pulse 1s infinite' : 'none'\n          }} />\n          <span style={{ color: '#06b6d4', fontSize: '0.9em' }}>\n            \ud83c\udfa4 {isListening ? 'LISTENING' : 'READY'}\n          </span>\n        </div>\n\n        {isListening && (\n          <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', gap: 3, height: 25, marginBottom: 10 }}>\n            {[...Array(12)].map((_, i) => (\n              <div key={i} style={{\n                width: 3, background: 'linear-gradient(to top, #10b981, #06b6d4)',\n                borderRadius: 2, animation: `wave 0.4s ${i * 0.05}s infinite alternate`, height: 8\n              }} />\n            ))}\n          </div>\n        )}\n\n        {transcript && (\n          <div style={{ background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)', borderRadius: 8, padding: 10, marginBottom: 12 }}>\n            <span style={{ color: '#10b981', fontSize: '0.75em' }}>\u2713 HEARD</span>\n            <p style={{ color: '#e2e8f0', margin: '4px 0 0' }}>\"{transcript}\"</p>\n          </div>\n        )}\n\n        <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', gap: 10 }}>\n          <button onClick={toggleListening} style={{\n            padding: '10px 24px', borderRadius: 25, border: 'none',\n            background: isListening ? Please enter your phone number.\\\");\\n  }, []);\\n\\n  // Voice recognition setup\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    const SR = (window as any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\\n    if (SR) {\\n      recognitionRef.current = new SR();\\n      recognitionRef.current.continuous = true;\\n      recognitionRef.current.interimResults = true;\\n      \\n      recognitionRef.current.onresult = (event: any) => {\\n        let text = '';\\n        for (let i = event.resultIndex; i < event.results.length; i++) {\\n          text += event.results[i][0].transcript;\\n        }\\n        setTranscript(text);\\n        \\n        if (event.results[event.resultIndex].isFinal) {\\n          processVoice(text);\\n        }\\n      };\\n    }\\n  }, []);\\n\\n  const processVoice = useCallback((text: string) => {\\n    const numberWords: Record<string, string> = {\\n      'zero': '0', 'one': '1', 'two': '2', 'three': '3', 'four': '4',\\n      'five': '5', 'six': '6', 'seven': '7', 'eight': '8', 'nine': '9', 'oh': '0'\\n    };\\n    \\n    let processed = text.toLowerCase();\\n    for (const [word, digit] of Object.entries(numberWords)) {\\n      processed = processed.replace(new RegExp(`\\\\\\\\b${word}\\\\\\\\b`, 'g'), digit);\\n    }\\n    \\n    const digits = processed.replace(/\\\\D/g, '');\\n    if (digits.length > 0) {\\n      const newPhone = (localPhone + digits).slice(0, 10);\\n      setLocalPhone(newPhone);\\n      onChange(newPhone);\\n      \\n      if (newPhone.length === 10) {\\n        speak(\\\"Phone number complete. Click Send OTP to continue.\\\");\\n      }\\n    }\\n  }, [localPhone, onChange, speak]);\\n\\n  const toggleListening = () => {\\n    if (isListening) {\\n      recognitionRef.current?.stop();\\n      setIsListening(false);\\n    } else {\\n      recognitionRef.current?.start();\\n      setIsListening(true);\\n    }\\n  };\\n\\n  const formatPhone = (p: string) => {\\n    if (p.length <= 3) return p;\\n    if (p.length <= 6) return `${p.slice(0,3)}-${p.slice(3)}`;\\n    return `${p.slice(0,3)}-${p.slice(3,6)}-${p.slice(6)}`;\\n  };\\n\\n  const handleChange = (value: string) => {\\n    const digits = value.replace(/\\\\D/g, '').slice(0, 10);\\n    setLocalPhone(digits);\\n    onChange(digits);\\n  };\\n\\n  const isValid = localPhone.length === 10;\\n\\n  return (\\n    <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', alignItems: 'center', gap: 20 }}>\\n      <span style={{ fontSize: '3em' }}>\\ud83c\\udfd7\\ufe0f</span>\\n      <h3 style={{ color: THEME.accent, margin: 0 }}>Builder Phone Number</h3>\\n      <p style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: '0.9em', margin: 0 }}>\\n        Say digits like \\\"seven zero three\\\" or type below\\n      </p>\\n\\n      <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 10 }}>\\n        <span style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: '1.2em' }}>+1</span>\\n        <input\\n          type=\\\"tel\\\"\\n          value={formatPhone(localPhone)}\\n          onChange={e => handleChange(e.target.value)}\\n          placeholder=\\\"000-000-0000\\\"\\n          style={{\\n            padding: '16px 20px',\\n            fontSize: '1.5em',\\n            fontFamily: 'monospace',\\n            background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)',\\n            border: `2px solid ${isValid ? '#10b981' : THEME.accent}40`,\\n            borderRadius: 12,\\n            color: '#fff',\\n            textAlign: 'center',\\n            width: 220,\\n            outline: 'none'\\n          }}\\n        />\\n      </div>\\n\\n      {/* Voice Bar */}\\n      <div style={{\\n        width: '100%',\\n        padding: 16,\\n        background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)',\\n        borderRadius: 16,\\n        border: `2px solid ${isListening ? '#10b981' : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)'}`\\n      }}>\\n        <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 10, marginBottom: 12 }}>\\n          <div style={{\\n            width: 10, height: 10, borderRadius: '50%',\\n            background: isListening ? '#10b981' : '#64748b',\\n            animation: isListening ? 'pulse 1s infinite' : 'none'\\n          }} />\\n          <span style={{ color: '#06b6d4', fontSize: '0.9em' }}>\\n            \\ud83c\\udfa4 {isListening ? 'LISTENING' : 'READY'}\\n          </span>\\n        </div>\\n\\n        {isListening && (\\n          <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', gap: 3, height: 25, marginBottom: 10 }}>\\n            {[...Array(12)].map((_, i) => (\\n              <div key={i} style={{\\n                width: 3, background: 'linear-gradient(to top, #10b981, #06b6d4)',\\n                borderRadius: 2, animation: `wave 0.4s ${i * 0.05}s infinite alternate`, height: 8\\n              }} />\\n            ))}\\n          </div>\\n        )}\\n\\n        {transcript && (\\n          <div style={{ background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)', borderRadius: 8, padding: 10, marginBottom: 12 }}>\\n            <span style={{ color: '#10b981', fontSize: '0.75em' }}>\\u2713 HEARD</span>\\n            <p style={{ color: '#e2e8f0', margin: '4px 0 0' }}>\\\"{transcript}\\\"</p>\\n          </div>\\n        )}\\n\\n        <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', gap: 10 }}>\\n          <button onClick={toggleListening} style={{\\n            padding: '10px 24px', borderRadius: 25, border: 'none',\\n            background: isListening ? '#ef4444' : '#10b981',\\n            color: 'white', fontWeight: 600, cursor: 'pointer'\\n          }}>\\n            {isListening ? '\\u23f9\\ufe0f Stop' : '\\ud83c\\udfa4 Listen'}\\n          </button>\\n        </div>\\n      </div>\\n\\n      <button\\n        onClick={onNext}\\n        disabled={!isValid}\\n        style={{\\n          padding: '14px 40px',\\n          background: isValid ? THEME.accent : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)',\\n          border: 'none',\\n          borderRadius: 30,\\n          color: isValid ? '#000' : '#666',\\n          fontSize: '1em',\\n          fontWeight: 600,\\n          cursor: isValid ? 'pointer' : 'not-allowed'\\n        }}\\n      >\\n        Send OTP \\u2192\\n      </button>\\n\\n      <style>{`\\n        @keyframes pulse { 0%,100%{opacity:1} 50%{opacity:0.5} }\\n        @keyframes wave { from{height:6px} to{height:20px} }\\n      `}</style>\\n    </div>\\n  );\\n};\\n\\nexport default BuilderPhone;\\nBUILDERPHONE\\n\\necho \\\"  \\u2705
